If we got back to the room at six o'clock, then Vicky waited for us for ten minutes; if we came back late, I think she could also be seen at the door of the room waiting for the guests. The coffee machine is a small part of the guest room, but she is willing to take responsibility for such a small thing, follow up continuously and care for the guests really makes us really admire and move. Although I haven't had much contact with her, her service is really impressive.
